### 4. 高级时尚超现实棋盘大片

**作者**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne/status/2039985799484358917)  **日期**: 2026-04-03  **语言**: en

> 一份详细的提示词，用于生成一张以特定年轻女性（通过参考图锁定身份）为主角的高级时尚概念摄影作品，场景置于超现实的棋盘环境中，配有超大号的亮面粉色和白色棋子，采用柔和的摄影棚光影及马卡龙色调。

![高级时尚超现实棋盘大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284633670_tdr9cb_HE98QFdasAAoElk.jpg)
![高级时尚超现实棋盘大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284633703_xpcphv_HE98Qr6aEAABb3k.jpg)
![高级时尚超现实棋盘大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284633716_jr75mq_HE98RMhaEAA-Wul.jpg)

```
A high-fashion conceptual lifestyle photograph of a young woman placed inside a surreal chessboard environment.
Use the provided reference image for the face and identity — strictly preserve exact facial structure, proportions, skin tone, eye color, and hair color. Do not alter identity, expression, or realism.
The scene features a large-scale black-and-white checkered floor resembling a chessboard, surrounded by oversized glossy chess pieces in soft pink and white tones. The chess pieces are tall, smooth, and reflective, creating a surreal, dreamlike atmosphere.
The woman is positioned slightly bent forward in a natural, interactive pose, gently touching or moving a large pink chess piece, as if engaged in a strategic moment. Her posture feels candid yet intentional.
Outfit: a soft pastel pink leather jacket layered over a clean white top, paired with a delicate, flowy white tulle skirt. Light pink heels complement the outfit, maintaining a cohesive monochrome aesthetic.
Hair & Styling: natural tied-back hairstyle with loose strands, soft makeup, clean and elegant look.
Lighting: soft studio lighting with diffused highlights, subtle reflections on glossy chess pieces, balanced shadows, high-end editorial lighting style.
Camera: top-down angled perspective (slightly elevated), 50mm lens, sharp focus on subject, geometric composition emphasizing symmetry and scale, background clean and controlled.
Style: high-fashion editorial, surreal luxury aesthetic, minimal yet bold composition, pastel color grading, Instagram-worthy artistic direction.
Quality: 8K, HDR, ultra-realistic, highly detailed textures, smooth skin tones, crisp focus, no distortion.
```

**作者**: [Puneet Kharbanda](https://x.com/KPuneet20/status/2038420352670326936)  **日期**: 2026-03-30  **语言**: en

> 这是一个高度具体的提示词，旨在生成一张用户在顶层公寓的超写实时尚大片（要求 100% 保留参考图的面部特征）。内容详细描述了人物的服装（黑色乳胶中长裙）、动作（水晶杯中溢出的香槟）、背景（雨夜城市）以及用于定格瞬间的复杂灯光和相机设置。

![顶层公寓超写实时尚大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774939641641_hjsaj9_HEnn_zCWYAAUUmj.jpg)

```
A hyper-realistic editorial shot of myself, keeping my exact face unchanged. IMPORTANT: Do not alter the face of the reference face; the output must have 100% exact facial features as the reference image. I am standing atop a plush emerald velvet stool in a high-rise penthouse, leaning slightly forward with a playful but sophisticated expression. In my right hand, I hold a vintage crystal flute as champagne overflows in mid-air, capturing every glistening droplet. I am wearing an asymmetrical black latex midi dress with structured, padded shoulders and a wide silver chain-link belt that cinches the waist. The background features floor-to-ceiling glass walls overlooking a rain-slicked city at night, with blurred neon lights creating a vibrant bokeh. The lighting is a mix of cool blue ambient tones from the city and warm, directional gold point lights from the interior chandeliers, creating a luxurious rim light. Shot on a 35mm f/1.4 lens with a fast shutter speed to freeze the liquid motion, ensuring pristine 8k clarity with no artifacts. Ensure the output maintains 100% exact facial features from the reference image; do not alter the face.
```

### 11. 高级时装 棚拍姿势 提示词 (绝对身份锁定)

**作者**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne/status/2037266255925924093)  **日期**: 2026-03-26  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的提示词，适用于 Nano Banana Pro，用于生成一张年轻女性的时尚大片。该女性在影棚环境中摆出特定姿势（四肢着地），要求绝对的身份一致性锁定、逼真的织物细节以及柔和、专业的影棚灯光。

![高级时装 棚拍姿势 提示词 (绝对身份锁定)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774594322374_l4crje_HEXS2y1bYAEUfkm.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman in a high-fashion studio pose, Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact",
      "identity_lock": "ABSOLUTE — Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact. Same face, same eyes, same proportions, same bone structure. Do NOT modify identity.",
      "pose": {
        "body_position": "on hands and knees on studio floor",
        "torso": "leaning forward at a low angle, spine slightly arched naturally",
        "hips": "raised slightly above shoulder level, natural alignment (no exaggeration)",
        "legs": "knees bent and resting on floor, lower legs angled backward",
        "arms": {
          "front_arm": "extended forward on floor with relaxed hand and naturally spread fingers",
          "rear_arm": "bent at elbow with hand raised near face"
        },
        "head": "tilted slightly downward and forward toward camera",
        "gaze": "directly at camera, intense editorial look",
        "expression": "soft parted lips, calm controlled expression"
      }
    },
    "hair": {
      "rule": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact",
      "style": "long straight hair falling forward over shoulders and partially onto floor",
      "details": "natural strands visible, slight separation of hair sections, realistic shine, no stylization"
    },
    "face": {
      "rule": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact",
      "eyes": "same eye color from reference image, sharp focus, natural reflections",
      "skin": "realistic skin texture with pores, no smoothing, no beautify",
      "lips": "natural texture, slightly parted, no artificial enhancement"
    },
    "attire": {
      "outfit": {
        "top": "black fitted top with thin straps, matte fabric",
        "bottom": "black short skirt or layered fabric with soft texture (non-transparent, non-explicit)",
        "legs": "sheer black tights with realistic stretch and slight sheen",
        "footwear": "black high heels with glossy finish"
      },
      "accessories": {
        "neck": "thin black choker",
        "wrists": "soft black textured cuffs or fabric accents",
        "headpiece": "subtle black decorative headband (minimal, non-costume exaggerated)"
      },
      "fabric_details": "realistic folds, compression, stretch, and contact shadows"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "professional studio",
      "background": "smooth seamless gradient backdrop (soft purple fading to neutral)",
      "floor": "clean matte studio floor with subtle soft shadow and slight reflection"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "setup": "studio 3-point lighting",

```
A high-fashion editorial triptych featuring a young French woman with a messy brunette bob and a natural smile. She is wearing a long, form-fitting knit dress with horizontal red and white stripes, paired with classic brown leather loafers and a vintage crossbody bag. The style is effortlessly elegant with a "je ne sais quoi" Parisian vibe.
​The Surreal Detail:
The focal point is the hem of the dress, which is visibly unraveled. A single, vibrant red thread of yarn has come loose and extends outward, trailing behind her along the cobblestone street like a thin, continuous line, connecting her to an unseen point in the distance.
​Setting & Atmosphere:
​Location: A narrow, historic street in Paris with beige stone buildings and a traditional "TABAC" brasserie in the background.
​Lighting: Soft, overcast daylight that brings out the richness of the red yarn and the texture of the cobblestones.
​Composition: A three-panel layout showing a close-up of the frayed hem, a full-length shot of her walking, and a medium shot focusing on her expression and the dress texture.

 },

### 34. Dusk Ascension JSON Prompt for Nano Banana Pro

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2031728499388543376)  **日期**: 2026-03-11  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro，定义了主体定位、梦幻空灵的超现实主义美学与复古奢华的编辑风格、星芒镜头光晕等特定光照效果、详细的色彩渐变调色板，以及用于图像生成的广泛负面约束。

![Dusk Ascension JSON Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773297027656_ivf33m_HDIl8OOa8AA3RcZ.jpg)
![Dusk Ascension JSON Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773297028228_wmox9t_HDIl8OaaYAAwblH.jpg)
![Dusk Ascension JSON Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773297028057_jiasi4_HDIl6IebkAACtuO.jpg)
![Dusk Ascension JSON Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773297029012_wae8ri_HDIl8OAXoAAjQtE.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject_settings": {
      "placeholder": "{argument name="subject" default="[SUBJECT GOES HERE]"}",
      "positioning": "absolute dead-center composition, full subject visibility, no clipping, no cutoff edges",
      "presentation": "floating mid-air, isolated, no pedestals, no stands, no display boxes, no mannequins"
    },
    "aesthetic_style": {
      "visual_theme": "dreamy ethereal surrealism, vintage luxury editorial, 1990s high-fashion film photography",
      "texture": "heavy analog film grain, noisy texture, slight motion blur, soft focus dream-haze, chromatic aberration",
      "lighting": "starburst lens flare on metallic highlights, soft glowing aura, backlit silhouette depth, no studio lights, no softboxes"
    },
    "color_palette": {
      "primary_gradient": {
        "top_color": "#1A3A5F",
        "middle_color": "#7B9BB9",
        "bottom_color": "#D4823B"
      },
      "description": "A seamless dusk-to-dawn transition from deep midnight blue to a warm, hazy amber sunset glow"
    },
    "negative_constraints": [
      "text",
      "watermarks",
      "studio equipment",
      "lighting stands",
      "reflectors",
      "frames",
      "borders",
      "cut off subject",
      "out of frame",
      "multiple subjects",
      "cluttered background",
      "plastic textures",
      "hyper-realistic digital sharpness",
      "clean 4k render"
    ],
    "technical_parameters": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "style_strength": "high",
      "diffusion_iteration": "film_emulsion_simulation"
    }
  }
}
```

### 36. 实验性纳米香蕉高级定制礼服提示

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2031045598519197855)  **日期**: 2026-03-09  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana 设计的实验性结构化提示，用于生成一件超逼真的高级定制晚礼服。它使用一个“TRANSFER_MATRIX”来定义设计元素（孔雀尾巴、彩色玻璃、玫瑰荆棘、冰柱），并使用一个“INSTRUCTION”在影棚灯光下构建一个既华丽又危险的廓形。

![实验性纳米香蕉高级定制礼服提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124334491_wv43ha_HC3KOcKW8AEBXUE.jpg)
![实验性纳米香蕉高级定制礼服提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124334691_cu0jh1_HC3KRKWaYAA-2MC.jpg)

```
TRANSFER_MATRIX:
peacock tail fan -> gown train expansion geometry
cathedral stained glass -> bodice panel segmentation
rose thorns -> silver embroidery edge logic
icicles -> earring taper logic

INSTRUCTION:
Build a haute couture evening gown using the transfer matrix above.
The silhouette must feel regal and dangerous, not costume-like.
Photorealistic luxury fashion editorial, studio lighting, black background.
```

  “meta”: {

### 44. 乌尔都语/英语 JSON 格式的详细时尚摄影提示

### 45. 时尚编辑网格提示（红色缎面心形眼镜）

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2028543120577855845)  **日期**: 2026-03-02  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一个 3x3 的时尚专题网格，其中包含一位成年女性，她在所有 9 个画面中都保持一致的身份。造型重点是红色缎面衬衫、牛仔裤和半透明红色心形太阳镜，并指定了现代时尚照明和各种姿势。

![时尚编辑网格提示（红色缎面心形眼镜）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772519717020_9bs5qn_HCbVJGPWkAAfUxa.jpg)

```
{
 "generation_request": {
 "meta_data": {
 "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
 "task_type": "editorial_pop_campaign_grid",
 "language": "en",
 "priority": "highest",
 "version": "v2.0_RED_SATIN_HEART_GLASSES_GRID"
 },

 "input": {
 "mode": "text_to_image",
 "notes": "Create a 3x3 fashion editorial grid featuring one adult woman with consistent identity across all 9 frames. High-fashion studio campaign style."
 },

 "output_settings": {
 "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
 "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
 "layout": {
 "type": "grid",
 "rows": 3,
 "cols": 3,
 "gutter": "thin",
 "outer_border": "none"
 },
 "render_style": "high_fashion_studio",
 "sharpness": "editorial_crisp",
 "grain": "none"
 },

 "scene": {
 "environment": "minimal studio with soft warm beige or light blush backdrop",
 "lighting": {
 "style": "modern fashion campaign lighting",
 "key_light": "large softbox front",
 "fill": "balanced soft fill",
 "shadow": "clean sculpted fashion shadow"
 },

### 53. 公园里时尚年轻女性的提示

**作者**: [𓆩𝐀𝐛𝐢𝐝 𝐇𝐮𝐬𝐬𝐚𝐢𝐧𓆪](https://x.com/AbidkingB/status/2027231370284818655)  **日期**: 2026-02-27  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，用于生成一张时尚年轻女性坐在宁静公园的深红色木凳上的图像。该提示强调柔和、梦幻般的自然日光、电影般的散景效果以及优雅休闲的服饰。

![公园里时尚年轻女性的提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772259938335_42hzoe_HCIsKhVb0AAI05-.jpg)

```
A fashionable young woman seated on a crimson-painted wooden bench in a peaceful outdoor park setting. The scene is illuminated by gentle natural daylight with a soft, dreamy shallow depth of field. She is dressed in an olive-toned casual sweatshirt with casually folded sleeves, paired with black distressed slim-fit jeans and light beige sneakers. Minimal yet elegant accessories — a delicate pendant necklace, a subtle bracelet, and a simple ring — enhance her look.
She sits in an easy, composed posture, leaning slightly forward while one hand rests casually along the bench, gazing at the camera with calm confidence. The background fades into an artistic blur of green trees and warm earthy tones, enhanced by a cinematic bokeh effect that adds depth and atmosphere.

### 62. 女性模特逼真时尚摄影提示词

**作者**: [Natty Windstorm](https://x.com/NattyWindstorm/status/2024479188485382360)  **日期**: 2026-02-19  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 格式提示，专为超逼真的时尚摄影设计，重点是一位纹身遍布全身的女性模特，身穿绿色几何图案比基尼，在豪华户外别墅露台上，正午刺眼的阳光下摆姿势。该提示详细说明了拍摄对象细节、环境、光线、相机设置和所需风格，旨在通过 Nano Banana Pro 呈现超现实、高分辨率的时尚大片。

![女性模特逼真时尚摄影提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771569149337_eqki0j_HBhkGbpXQAA6NIr.jpg)
![女性模特逼真时尚摄影提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771569149373_r1addn_HBhkGbpXkAANOiD.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "photorealistic_fashion_photography",
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "appearance": {
      "hair": "long platinum blonde hair, loose waves",
      "skin": "light tan skin",
      "body_type": "slim, curvy, athletic",
      "tattoos": "extensive floral and ornamental tattoos covering arms, legs, and torso",
      "expression": "confident, relaxed, slightly serious",
      "pose": "reclining sideways on a circular outdoor lounge chair, leaning on one arm with legs extended"
    },
    "clothing": {
      "outfit": "{argument name="bikini color and pattern" default="green geometric patterned bikini"}",
      "accessories": [
        "small narrow sunglasses"
      ]
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "luxury modern outdoor villa terrace",
    "furniture": "round wicker daybed with beige cushion and pillows",
    "background": [
      "minimalist concrete walls",
      "glass railing",
      "lush tropical plants",
      "clear blue sky"
    ],
    "props": [
      "green patterned fabric draped on chair"
    ]
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural sunlight",
    "quality": "bright, harsh midday sun",
    "shadows": "sharp realistic shadows",
    "direction": "direct overhead sunlight"
  },
  "camera": {
    "angle": "eye level",
    "framing": "full body shot",
    "lens": "85mm lens",
    "depth_of_field": "moderate depth of field, subject in sharp focus, slightly softened background"
  },
  "style": {
    "photorealism": "ultra realistic",
    "resolution": "high resolution, 8k",
    "quality": "professional fashion editorial",
    "color": "natural color grading, warm tones",
    "texture": "detailed skin texture, fabric texture, wicker texture"
  },
  "mood": "luxury, relaxed, confident, summer lifestyle",
  "render_settings": {
    "sharpness": "high",
    "contrast": "medium high",
    "saturation": "natural",
    "noise": "none"
  }
}
```

### 64. 覆盆子光泽微距编辑网格提示

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2024137074639598040)  **日期**: 2026-02-18  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一个 2x2 的美妆专题微距网格，其中包含同一位女性模特，重点突出光泽感唇部和眼部，使用覆盆子作为性感的道具，并在所有面板中保持一致的身份和高端摄影美学。

![覆盆子光泽微距编辑网格提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771483135561_1fb1oa_HBct4HuWEAErDON.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "beauty_editorial_macro_series_grid",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_RASPBERRY_GLOSS_MACRO_EDITORIAL_GRID"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "text_to_image",
      "notes": "Create a 2x2 beauty editorial grid featuring the same adult female model. Each panel is a slightly different macro crop: (A) eye + cheek + lips with raspberry near mouth, (B) extreme close-up of glossy lips with raspberry touching the upper lip, (C) another extreme close-up from a slightly different angle, (D) eye + cheek + lips again with a micro-variation in gaze and raspberry placement. Keep identity, makeup, and styling consistent across all panels. No text, no logos."
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin"
      },
      "sharpness": "editorial_crisp",
      "grain": "subtle_film",
      "post_processing": {
        "skin_retouch": "light_editorial",
        "texture_preservation": "high",
        "avoid_plastic_skin": true,
        "avoid_hdr": true
      }
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "high-fashion beauty editorial macro campaign with raspberries as a sensual prop",
      "environment": "minimal studio, warm neutral background, no visible set elements",
      "composition": {
        "framing": "macro close-ups, tight crops, emphasis on lips and eye",
        "camera_height": "eye_level",
        "focus_priority": "lips_texture_and_gloss_highlights"
      },
      "lighting": {
        "type": "soft_directional_studio_light",
        "direction": "slightly_side",
        "contrast": "medium_soft",
        "temperature": "warm_neutral",
        "highlight_behavior": "controlled_specular_on_gloss",
        "shadow_behavior": "soft_falloff"
      },
      "camera": {
        "look": "beauty_campaign_photography",
        "lens": "100mm_macro",
        "aperture": "f2.8",
        "depth_of_field": "shallow_but_legible",
        "macro_detail": "high"
      }
    },
    "subject": {
      "person": "adult woman",
      "appearance": {
        "skin": "natural pores visible, faint freckles, soft warm undertone",
        "hair": "straight dark hair, sleek, partially framing face",
        "eye_color": "hazel_or_brown"
      },
      "makeup": {
        "complexion": "light foundation with natural texture, soft powder control",
        "blush": "dusty_rose blush on cheekbones",
        "eyes": "sharp winged eyeliner, long separated lashes, subtle shimmer on lids",
        "lips": "deep berry red lipstick with high gloss finish, crisp lip line, visible lip texture"
      },
      "props": {
        "raspberries": "fresh raspberries placed near and touching the lips, one held between fingers",
        "hands": "fingers in frame holding raspberry,
```

 },

### 68. 奢华护肤品：香水瓶中的立体模型

**作者**: [Willy](https://x.com/jw660227/status/2023740007689965712)  **日期**: 2026-02-17  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、高级定制风格的提示，用于生成一张奢华护肤精华液微缩景观的微距照片，其中有微型韩国女音乐家和一位指挥家在香奈儿五号香水瓶内的精华液池中表演。

![奢华护肤品：香水瓶中的立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771396569473_xvzwoz_HBXEy1DagAE3HcP.jpg)

```
Luxury skincare serum diorama
LAYOUT: Single hero, miniature concert hall within a perfume bottle
DIRECTION: Vertical, rising elegance, intricate details
BACKGROUND: Opulent miniature concert hall, velvet textures, soft bokeh
PRODUCT: Voluptuous Korean woman conductors and musicians in shimmering couture performing in a serum pool within the perfume bottle, porcelain skin, long silky hair, sultry gazes, graceful poses, jeweled instruments
DYNAMIC: Cascading serum droplets, floating musical notes, subtle mist
TONE: Tone-on-tone, blush rose and champagne gold palette
STYLE: Soft, luxurious, K-beauty aesthetic, macro photography, couture fashion editorial
MAIN ELEMENT:
A scaled-down world inside a Chanel No. 5 perfume bottle, crystal-clear serum forming a pool, miniature rose bushes and glowing flora, miniature musicians playing harps, violins, and cellos, and a woman conductor standing poised.
DYNAMIC ELEMENTS:
Droplets of serum cascading like waterfalls, musical notes gently floating, subtle golden mist adding a magical touch, fabric flow from the silk gowns.
CAMERA: Shot on Hasselblad X2D, 85mm f/1.2, Rembrandt lighting, shallow depth of field.
Style keywords: enchanting, voluptuous, luxurious, K-beauty, miniature, diorama, couture.
```

### 72. 前卫路易威登滑雪镜编辑提示

**作者**: [Meem](https://x.com/mehvishs25/status/2022870353018786081)  **日期**: 2026-02-15  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张前卫路易威登（Louis Vuitton）风格滑雪镜的高级时尚编辑照片，强调高对比度的明暗对照（Chiaroscuro）光线、金属细节和深色背景。

> 一个复杂的 JSON 提示，专为图像到图像生成而设计，用于创建四格工作室时尚画册网格。该提示严格要求保留参考图像中的面部特征，同时生成一位女性穿着象牙色雪纺露背迷你连衣裙在柔和的编辑灯光下的四种不同姿势。

    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "studio_fashion_editorial_lookbook_quad_pose",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.1_IVORY_CHIFFON_HALTER_LOOKBOOK_GRID_FACE_MATCH"

    },
    "output": {

      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin"
      },
      "sharpness": "high",
      "grain": "subtle_analog"
    },

      "environment": "clean off-white studio wall backdrop, seamless floor, neutral studio setting, no clutter",
      "mood": "elegant, airy, understated, high-end boutique lookbook"
    },
    "subject": {
      "person": "adult woman",
      "identity_consistency": "model across all panels",
      "face_match": "very_high lips",
      "expression": "calm, slightly sultry, neutral editorial gaze",
      "hair": "long dark hair, soft waves, center part (similar to reference), tidy and glossy; allow subtle variation but keep overall match",
      "makeup": "soft neutral glam, defined eyeliner, natural nude lips (match reference makeup vibe)",
      "accessories": "small gold hoop earrings, delicate rings/bracelet",
      "wardrobe": {
        "dress": "ivory / champagne chiffon halter mini dress with high neck band, airy layered bubble hem, semi-sheer flowing fabric, open back with long scarf-like tie draping down"
      },
      "shoes": "minimal strappy heels or sandals in nude/ivory"
    },
    "poses_grid": {
      "panel_1_top_left": "front 3/4 pose, one arm bent with hand resting near neck, relaxed posture",

```

  },

### 104. 时尚编辑联系表（3x3 网格）

**作者**: [Sandy](https://x.com/Sandykabariya/status/2018551584029020279)  **日期**: 2026-02-03  **语言**: en

> 一个旨在生成 3x3 网格格式的时尚编辑联系表的提示。主题是一位留着利落黑色波波头的现代女性，身穿米色定制西装，戴着白色椭圆形太阳镜，在极简主义工作室中拍摄。核心指令是展示不同角度（正面、侧面、俯视），主体反复伸向相机，以营造强烈的景深和透视畸变效果。

![时尚编辑联系表（3x3 网格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187154579_kisfcb_HANV9hpaYAA7pMg.jpg)

```
Editorial fashion contact sheet of a modern woman with a sharp black bob haircut wearing white oval sunglasses, a beige tailored suit over a red sweater vest and white shirt, photographed in a minimalist studio with a neutral grey backdrop. Multiple frames arranged in a 3×3 grid showing varied angles—front, side, top-down, back view—while the subject repeatedly reaches her hand toward the camera lens, creating strong depth and perspective distortion. Clean high-fashion styling, bold color contrast, soft diffused studio lighting, crisp focus, contemporary magazine aesthetic, 35mm–50mm look, ultra-sharp, high resolution.
```

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张安娜·德·阿玛斯（Ana de Armas）的奢华时尚照片，重点突出鲜明、高饱和度的抖音网红美学。该提示详细说明了她的姿势（坐在石质栏杆上）、服装（勃艮第酒红色天鹅绒迷你连衣裙和及膝靴）以及精致的妆容（玻璃肌、漫画睫毛、樱桃红唇），背景设定在欧洲古典别墅露台，沐浴在明亮的自然阳光下。

![Ana de Armas 奢华时尚摄影提示词（抖音风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668450980_7x4yfz_G_wvT8TWsAAbzcZ.jpg)
![Ana de Armas 奢华时尚摄影提示词（抖音风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668450968_mdov36_G_wvTWObwAEn75X.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_parameters": {
    "global_metadata": {
      "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
      "style_preset": "Luxury Fashion Photography",
      "aesthetic_target": "Douyin-Influencer / Modern Editorial",
      "color_profile": "High Saturation / Vivid"
    },
    "subject": {
      "identity_fidelity": {
        "primary_likeness": "Ana de Armas",
        "constraints": "Strictly preserve original facial features; no AI-morphing"
      },
      "physique": {
        "pose": "Seated sideways on a stone balustrade; diagonal orientation",
        "modifications": "Enhanced bust silhouette; deep V-neckline focus"
      },
      "cosmetics_douyin_style": {
        "skin": "Luminous 'glass skin'; localized high-shine highlighter",
        "eyes": "Pinkish-red eyeshadow; individual manga-style lash clusters",
        "lips": "High-gloss cherry-red finish; defined borders"
      },
      "hairstyling": {
        "base": "Long, straight auburn hair; high-gloss finish",
        "arrangement": "Half-up ponytail; dual face-framing strands",
        "accents": "Gold-toned hair clips; delicate metallic beads"
      }
    },
    "apparel_system": {
      "primary_garment": {
        "item": "Sleeveless mini dress",
        "color": "Deep Burgundy",
        "material": "Velvet with subtle leopard-print texture",
        "architecture": {
          "top": "Halter neck; deep V-plunge; open back",
          "bottom": "Layered ruffled hem; high-volume texture"
        }
      },
      "footwear": {
        "item": "Knee-high boots",
        "color": "Matching Burgundy",
        "finish": "Sleek/Polished"
      }
    },
    "environment_architecture": {

      "midground": "Old stone castle masonry (right-side frame)",
      "background": {
        "landscape": "Green valley panorama; mist-covered mountain range",

### 121. Alexander McQueen 运动鞋编辑网格提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro

**作者**: [摆烂程序媛](https://x.com/wanerfu/status/2016361603260940371)  **日期**: 2026-01-28  **语言**: zh

> 一个高度详细、专业级的提示，用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 工具，旨在创建一个以 Alexander McQueen 男士奢侈运动鞋为中心的 3x3 编辑联系表网格。该提示指定了九个独特的视觉概念、严格的产品一致性、光照、风格（Vogue/GQ 美学）和技术参数（8K 分辨率、高动态范围）。

![Alexander McQueen 运动鞋编辑网格提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668517208_7c2eeo_G_uOL8mbAAEHFtE.jpg)

```
为高端商业营销活动创建3×3网格，以Alexander McQueen男士奢侈运动鞋为中心主题。

每帧展现独特视觉概念，同时保持九张图像中完美的产品一致性。

网格概念（每格一个）：

1. '标志性英雄镜头'：深色光滑基座上的眼平面侧视图，强调标志性超大鞋底。

2. '极致微距细节'：鞋跟或缝线特写，突显顶级皮革纹理和'Alexander McQueen'标志压纹。

3. '动态交互'：鞋踏上表面产生微妙优雅的黑色液体或大理石粉溅洒效果。

4. '极简雕塑感'：鞋艺术性地平衡在几何混凝土或大理石块上，强调建筑设计。

5. '悬浮轻盈感'：鞋悬浮空中，鞋带动态悬挂，传达顶级舒适感和轻盈感。

6. '感官质地'：聚焦天鹅绒或光滑皮革上部与粗糙石头纹理对比的触感氛围镜头。

7. '单色奢华'：背景与鞋的强调色完美匹配的色块场景，营造大胆编辑感。

8. '解构工艺'：原始材料的抽象排列（皮革样本、橡胶纹理）环绕鞋子，象征高质量构造。

9. '超现实融合'：鞋融入超现实梦幻景观，融合现实主义与高级时尚。

视觉规则：
* '主体'：Alexander McQueen男士超大运动鞋。
* '一致性'：鞋的形状、比例、鞋底厚度、标志位置和排版必须100%准确。
* '无扭曲'：标志性鞋底或品牌无变形。
* '分离'：鞋与背景清晰分离。

灯光与风格：
* 柔和受控的工作室灯光，具有戏剧性边光突显鞋的轮廓。
* 皮革上的细微高光，鞋底下深层逼真阴影。
* 高动态范围，8K分辨率，超锐利焦点。
* 编辑奢侈时尚广告美学（Vogue/GQ风格）。
* 调色板：极简主义、单色、金属和深哑光色调。

整体氛围：
* 现代、精致、视觉连贯。
* 奢侈时尚品牌高端商业活动。
* 超现实、电影感、精致和渴望感。
```

Create a high-fashion editorial look featuring a woman wearing a strapless sheer corset gown, also known as an illusion lace evening gown. The dress has a nude skin-tone base with intricate {argument name="lace color" default="black"} lace embroidery layered over transparent fabric. The corset-style bodice includes visible boning that cinches and shapes the waist, while the strapless neckline highlights the shoulders and collarbone. A dramatic {argument name="train color" default="black"} tulle train or skirt is attached at the back, adding volume, movement, and elegance to the silhouette. The overall aesthetic is luxurious, refined, and couture-focused, emphasizing structure, transparency, and contrast between nude fabric and black detailing.

> 一个高度详细的图像生成提示，用于拍摄一张社论时尚照片，照片中有两位模特（灵感来自安娜·德·阿玛斯 [Ana De Armas] 和西德尼·斯威尼 [Sydney Sweeney]），置身于一个奢华的步入式衣帽间。该提示详细说明了 Y2K 美学、高对比度闪光摄影和强烈的鱼眼镜头畸变，并详细描述了模特的姿势、服装（石灰绿色和天蓝色紧身胸衣连衣裙）以及环境（红色货架、芥末黄色地毯、名牌手袋）。

      "clean contemporary layout"

**作者**: [KeorUnreal](https://x.com/KeorUnreal/status/2013683690463772771)  **日期**: 2026-01-20  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂、结构化的提示，用于生成一张西德尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 的高级时装编辑图片，用于香水广告。场景设定在一个异想天开的粉彩红色糖果店，她正爬着一个质朴的木梯，身穿红黑千鸟格粗花呢西装外套和迷你裙，强调一种娇媚的“糖果核心”美学，呈现 4K 逼真画质。

![悉尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 在糖果店拍摄的高级时尚大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977332477_nu117h_G_IKozjX0AACdW-.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "name": "{argument name="subject name" default="Sydney Sweeney"}",
      "appearance": {
        "hair": "Long, flowing honey-blonde straight hair style",
        "expression": "Playful, alluring gaze with mouth slightly open",
        "makeup": "Soft glam, rosy cheeks, red glossy lips, defined lashes"
      },
      "outfit": {
        "top": "Red and black checkered/houndstooth tweed cropped blazer with long sleeves and three large pearl buttons",
        "bottom": "Matching red and black checkered/houndstooth high-waisted tweed adherent miniskirt and black fishnets",
        "footwear": "Light red patent leather pointed-toe stiletto pumps with signature red soles (Christian Louboutin)"
      },
      "pose": "Climbing a wooden ladder, body turned sideways to the camera, looking back over the left shoulder, left leg straight on a lower rung, right leg bent with foot placed on a higher rung, left hand holding the ladder side, right hand reaching out towards a shelf"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Whimsical pastel red candy shop",

### 157. 空姐私人飞机手机摄影专题

**作者**: [Maya](https://x.com/mayadelmare/status/2013382894891212811)  **日期**: 2026-01-19  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的手机摄影图像（iPhone 15 Pro Max 风格），内容是一位丰满的空姐在机场停机坪上，一架私人飞机旁。提示中详细说明了她的着装（海军蓝铅笔裙，隐约可见的蕾丝比基尼上衣）、动态姿势、强烈的午后阳光以及一种随性的社交媒体美学。

![空姐私人飞机手机摄影专题](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890658898_88efkj_G_D49X3W4AAqNyk.jpg)
![空姐私人飞机手机摄影专题](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890658913_ku55jm_G_D49XqWgAApZv8.jpg)

```
[
  {
    "metadata": {
      "title": "Stewardess Private Jet Editorial",
      "style": "Hyper-Realistic Mobile Photography",
      "target_device": "iPhone 15 Pro Max"
    },
    "subject": {
      "age": "Mid-30s",
      "ethnicity": "Caucasian/Mediterranean mix",
      "hair": {
        "style": "Long ombre waves",
        "color": "Brunette roots transitioning to sun-kissed blonde tips",
        "texture": "Voluminous and soft"
      },
      "physique": {
        "body_type": "Fit voluptuous hourglass",
        "bust": "Full natural volume, prominent cleavage",
        "features": "Deeply curved hips, toned waist, radiant skin texture"
      },
      "makeup": "Light natural aesthetic, soft mascara, nude lip gloss, subtle glowy highlighter",
      "expression": "Confident, alluring, slight playful smile"
    },
    "pose": {
      "description": "Dynamic 'girl pose'",
      "hand_placement": {
        "right_hand": "Firmly on the waist to accentuate hip curve",
        "left_hand": "Raised gracefully above her head, fingers slightly spread"
      },
      "posture": "Weight shifted to one leg, slight arch in the back"
    },

The rich red fabric appears silky and luxurious, catching light beautifully and adding depth and saturation to the scene.

The woman is lounging gracefully inside a large cream-colored hanging rattan cocoon chair, suspended gently, its woven texture adding a natural, bohemian element. Her posture is relaxed and poised, body slightly reclined, hands resting naturally, radiating effortless elegance. The setting is a modern boho-chic interior featuring neutral tones, soft textiles, natural wood, and organic materials, minimal yet stylish, enhancing the subject without distraction.

Lighting is golden hour side lighting, warm and directional, casting gentle shadows across her face and body, highlighting skin texture, fabric folds, and the woven chair. The atmosphere feels cinematic and intimate, like a high-end fashion film still. The color palette emphasizes rich saturated reds contrasted against soft creams and warm neutrals. Shot with shallow depth of field for a dreamy background blur, ultra-detailed, hyper-realistic, high fashion editorial quality, masterpiece, 8k resolution.

- She wears a cream silk power suit with clean lines and wide-leg trousers, paired with a delicate layered silver necklace. A designer clutch rests on the marble cafe table beside a steaming cup of matcha latte.

- Text Block: "{argument name="Text Block 1" default="Our Journey: A fusion of heritage and innovation, crafted for the modern woman."}"

- Image: Close-up beauty shot showcasing the glass skin effect and delicate jewelry.

- Text Block: "{argument name="Text Block 2" default="Commitment to quality, sustainability, and empowering women through fashion."}"

SECTION 6:
- Text Block: "Designed in Paris, inspired by the world."

Subtle motion blur as she turns her head slightly with gentle head tilt, soft contemplative expression, steam rising from the matcha latte cup creating warmth and atmosphere.
CAMERA: Hasselblad X2D, 85mm f/1.4 lens, soft diffused golden hour lighting, shallow depth of field, beauty retouching with luminous skin detail.
STYLE: Parisian elegance, power dressing, luxury fashion, ethereal Eurasian beauty, golden hour, warm and cool color palette, high-end fashion editorial.

A stylish handwritten signature "Willy" is elegantly placed in small letters at the Bottom Right corner.

A 3D miniature Zootopia visualization, no human model, showcasing seven artistic miniature stages: bustling Zootopia streets kissed by sunrise, tiny animal citizens harvesting carrots, dimly lit underground tunnels with precise rows of produce crates, intimate city cafe gatherings, ethereal misty morning savanna ambiance. Each tier displays district name, population percentage, and Zootopia Gazette tasting notes designed like precious gems. Backdrop evokes an expensive city hall setting, utilizing strong chiaroscuro lighting to create a high-fashion editorial ambiance. Shot with Hasselblad H6D-100c, 100mm f/2.2, extremely shallow depth of field with exquisite bokeh. Holographic displays of carrot cake pairing suggestions drift subtly, featuring artisanal cheese pairings for whites, intense dark chocolate for reds. The color story shifts from deep earth tones and jewel tones for full-bodied wines to icy greens, silvery golds, and champagne hues for crisp varietals.

      }
    },

        "framing": "Extreme Close-up (Eyes to Chin).",
        "action": "Holding a dark red rose against the cheek/jawline.",
        "expression": " intense, melancholic gaze, slightly parted lips.",
        "lighting": "Soft shadow on the left side of the face."
      },
      "panel_2_middle": {
        "framing": "Full Body / Wide Shot.",
        "pose": "Sitting on the floor with legs spread slightly (V-shape), knees bent. Hands resting in lap holding the rose stem vertically.",
        "posture": "Upright torso, elegant ballerina posture.",
        "background": "Solid black void."
      },

      }
    },

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，与另一个条目高度相似，用于生成一张高端商业生活方式照片。它严格要求保留参考图像中服装的精确细节，照片中一位白人美国女性模特以自然、自信的姿势置身于户外城市人行道场景中，沐浴在柔和的自然日光下。

        "visible natural pores",
        "light blemishes and imperfections",
        "soft expression lines around eyes/mouth",
        "light freckles across nose/cheeks",
        "natural skin highlights and subsurface scattering"
      ],
      "makeup": "minimal, natural or bare skin look"
    },

      "source": "garment_from_input_reference_image",
      "preservation_rules": [
        "exact color dye and pattern",
        "exact fabric weave and texture",
        "exact thread stitching details",
        "exact fit, drape, and silhouette on the body"
      ],
      "modification_permission": "NONE"
    },
    "pose": {
      "framing": "full_body_standing",
      "style": "natural, relaxed, confident",
      "orientation": "facing camera to showcase garment front"
    }
  },
  "environment_definition": {

    "contextual_logic": "architecture and decor must visually complement the style of the reference clothing",

      "textured building materials (brick, stone, wood)",
      "cafe seating or planter boxes",
      "pavement textures"
    ]
  },
  "composition_and_layout": {
    "camera_principles": [
      "commercial fashion standards",
      "golden ratio alignment of subject",
      "product-centered focus",
      "grid alignment"
    ],
    "framing_scale": "wide full shot (head to toe)",
    "spatial_margins": {

    }
  },

    "shadows": "clean, natural falloff defining form without harshness"
  },

    ]

### 175. 商业时尚摄影与严格的服装保护

**作者**: [Amanpreet Singh](https://x.com/amanxdesign/status/2011294705762648397)  **日期**: 2026-01-14  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张高端商业生活方式照片。核心指令是严格保留参考图像中服装的精确细节（颜色、图案、纹理、合身度），将主体（一位白人美国女模特）置于户外城市人行道场景中，摆出自然、放松的姿势，并辅以柔和的自然日光。

    "aesthetic": "high_end_fashion_campaign",

  },
  "subject_definition": {
    "identity": {
      "demographic": "white American female",
      "physique": "fit",
      "appearance": "beautiful, naturally styled"
    },
    "skin_and_features": {
      "realism_rule": "macro_level_human_realism; NO artificial smoothing or filtering",
      "texture_details": [
        "visible natural pores",
        "light blemishes and imperfections",
        "soft expression lines",
        "light freckles across nose/cheeks",
        "natural skin highlights"
      ],
      "makeup": "minimal, natural or bare skin look"
    },
    "attire_constraints": {
      "source": "garment_from_input_reference_image",

### 179. 美食视频的神奇转换提示词编译器（系统提示）

**作者**: [Emily](https://x.com/IamEmily2050/status/2011093173821714761)  **日期**: 2026-01-13  **语言**: en

> 一个高度复杂、多层次的系统提示，被设计为“魔法转换提示编译器”，用于生成 AI 驱动的食物转换视频。它概述了核心原则，例如关注点分离、像素主权（定义锁定区、转换区和瞬态区），以及体积和状态变化的物理合理性规则。这是一个元提示结构，旨在指导为各种图像和视频模型的多阶段工作流生成特定的机器提示。

```
# MAGICAL TRANSFORMATION PROMPT COMPILER v4.0 (Part 1 of 2)
# Production-Grade Latent Trajectory Generator

system_identity:
  name: "Magical Transformation Prompt Compiler"
  version: "4.0"
  role: >
    You are a precision prompt architect for AI-generated food transformation videos. 
    You produce complete, production-ready specification documents that include operator 
    instructions, machine prompts, and failure suppression layers. Your outputs are used 
    by professional AI artists running multi-stage workflows across image generators 
    (Midjourney, DALL-E, Flux) and video models (Veo3, Kling, Runway).

# CORE PRINCIPLES
core_principles:
  separation_of_concerns:
    description: "Distinct output types for different consumers"
    layers:
      - name: "OPERATOR INSTRUCTIONS"
        purpose: "Human-readable workflow guidance"
        format: "Step-by-step procedural text"
      - name: "MACHINE PROMPTS"
        purpose: "Copy-paste ready AI prompts"
        format: "Quoted prompt blocks with **PROMPT:** prefix"
      - name: "NEGATIVE PROMPTS"
        purpose: "Failure mode suppression"
        format: "Comma-separated exclusion terms"

  pixel_sovereignty:
    description: "Every pixel belongs to exactly ONE zone"
    zones:
      - name: "LOCKED"
        definition: "Immutable across all frames"
        examples: ["table surface", "container exterior", "shadows", "frame edges"]
      - name: "TRANSFORM"
        definition: "Changes between Frame A and Frame B"
        examples: ["container interior", "ingredients", "liquid level"]
      - name: "TRANSIENT"
        definition: "Exists only in video bridge"
        examples: ["motion blur", "steam during reveal", "hand movement"]

  physical_plausibility:
    description: "Transformations must obey observable physics"
    rules:
      - "Volume conservation with specified percentage change"
      - "Mass-energy consistency (cooking typically reduces volume)"
      - "Gravity compliance (no floating elements)"
      - "Temporal logic (effects follow causes, never precede)"
      - "State changes must be chemically plausible"

# INPUT SCHEMA
input_schema:
  required_parameters:
    concept:
      type: "string"
      description: "Name of the dish or transformation"
      examples: ["Beef Bourguignon", "Sushi Platter", "Korean Army Stew"]

  optional_parameters:
    cuisine_context:
      cuisine_origin:
        type: "string"
        description: "Cultural origin informing aesthetic defaults"
        examples: ["French", "Japanese", "Korean", "Italian", "Mexican"]
        inference_rule: "If not provided, infer from concept name"
      
      cooking_method:
        type: "string"
        description: "Primary cooking technique"
        examples: ["braised", "grilled", "fried", "steamed", "raw assembly"]
        inference_rule: "Infer from concept if not specified"

    transform_class:
      type: "enu
```

**作者**: [Willy](https://x.com/jw660227/status/2009938444924129588)  **日期**: 2026-01-10  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于生成不对称的专题版面（1 张大型主图，2 张堆叠的辅助图片），内容是一款美妆产品（口红）。美学风格为“暗黑奢华混搭”，带有华丽的魅力，背景是深勃艮第色天鹅绒，采用伦勃朗布光。它详细描述了主要拍摄对象（一位欧亚女性，湿润、有光泽的深红色嘴唇）以及产品的微距特写镜头。

![不对称暗黑奢华美妆专题报道](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143845321_th1s2x_G-S8XC7asAIk2FE.jpg)

```
Asymmetrical editorial spread, 4:5 ratio.

LAYOUT: Irregular grid (1+2) - large hero (60%) left, two supporting images (20% each) stacked right
DIRECTION: None (editorial arrangement)
BACKGROUND: Deep burgundy velvet, single spotlight, Rembrandt lighting
PRODUCT: Hero - A glamorous Eurasian woman with wet, glossy dark red lips and dewy skin poses seductively in a burgundy velvet dress, dramatic rim lighting; Supporting 1 - Close up of blood-red glossy lipstick being applied with a brush; Supporting 2 - Lipstick tube lying on a dark velvet surface with scattered crimson glitter.
DYNAMIC: Subtle glitter particles floating around the lipstick and model - subtle intensity.
TONE: Brand monochrome - deep burgundy, wine red, crimson
STYLE: Dark luxury hybrid, opulent glamour
HERO CELL (left 60%): Seductive woman, hourglass figure, wet lips, intense sultry gaze
SUPPORTING CELL 1 (top right, 20%): Macro shot, extreme close-up, product texture
SUPPORTING CELL 2 (bottom right, 20%): Product flat lay, moody dark velvet surface
TYPOGRAPHY: Elegant serif, high contrast, gold foil effect on headlines
CAMERA: Hasselblad H6D, 85mm f/1.2, shallow depth of field, Rembrandt lighting
Style keywords: Opulent beauty, velvet, glossy lips, high fashion, dramatic lighting. A stylish handwritten signature {argument name="signature name" default="Willy"} is elegantly and small letters placed at the Bottom Right corner

    },

  },

    "stance": "Full-body standing shot, facing directly forward",
    "posture": "Upright, legs straight, arms relaxed at sides",
    "expression": "Calm, confident, soft gaze"
  },
  "environment": {

### 184. Moody Fashion Editorial Rainy Night Prompt

**作者**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc/status/2009277072263279084)  **日期**: 2026-01-08  **语言**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，用于拍摄一张在雨夜中，情绪化、高对比度的时尚编辑快照，强调未经编辑的原始真实感和强烈的智能手机闪光效果。它包括生物保真度（皮肤物理、毳毛）、服装张力（皮夹克和超短裙）以及环境细节（雨滴和樱花清晰对焦）的详细说明。

![Moody Fashion Editorial Rainy Night Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967403896_yq0vph_G-Ji2NVXEAA_I4X.jpg)

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast [Moody Fashion Editorial] snapshot taken with an iPhone 17 Pro on a rainy night. DIRECT HARD SMARTPHONE FLASH. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus from the frozen raindrops to the distant blossoms.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" night hydration (mixed with rainwater), and a healthy cold-induced rosy flush on the cheeks. Fine vellus hair is visible along the jawline.
Hair: Wet-look chestnut hair, slightly wavy and clumping naturally into strands that frame her face and neck.
Silhouette Calibration: Amplify the dominant structural bust volume and the substantial, thick-toned leg presence. Focus on the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist, highlighted by the cropped fit of the jacket.
Outfit & Textural Interaction:

Clothing: A minimalist {argument name="jacket color" default="Chocolate Brown"} Leather Moto Jacket (worn slightly open) and a matching High-Waisted Leather Micro-Mini Skirt.
Tension: The stiff leather shows extreme material tension over her fit form, with realistic micro-cracks in the grain and high-key highlights from the flash.
Matter Physics: The subject holds a transparent clear umbrella covered in heavy, crystalline raindrops. The flash freezes the "story" of every drop in mid-air.
Pose & Composition:

Pose: Standing outdoors under a blooming cherry blossom tree. She is leaning slightly toward the lens, reaching one hand out to touch the edge of the umbrella, creating a sense of intimate depth and anatomical volume.
Perspective: Handheld smartphone POV, captured at a medium-distance to showcase her fit silhouette and the atmospheric environment.
Environment & Lighting:

Lighting: Hard Direct Smartphone Flash. The flash creates a brilliant "halo" effect on the wet cherry blossoms and reflects intensely off the transparent umbrella, casting a sharp, pitch-black shadow of her form into the dark night.
Background (SHARP): A dark, moody outdoor setting. The detailed textures of the pink cherry blossoms, the wet asphalt of the street, and the distant streetlights are all perfectly IN FOCUS. No artificial blur.
Quality: Raw unedited social-media leak aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows (ISO 1600 style), 8k resolution.
```

**Related**: [[科技产品]]、[[奇幻世界]]

{
  "task_configuration": {
    "type": "GENERATE",
    "sub_type": "commercial_lifestyle_photograph",
    "reference_logic": "STRICT_GARMENT_PRESERVATION_FROM_INPUT",
    "aesthetic": "high_end_fashion_campaign",
    "output_quality": "high_resolution_photorealistic"
  },
  "subject_definition": {

      "demographic": "white American female model",
      "physique": "fit",
      "appearance": "beautiful, naturally styled"
    },

        "visible natural pores",
        "light blemishes and imperfections",
        "soft expression lines around eyes/mouth",
        "light freckles across nose/cheeks",
        "natural skin highlights and subsurface scattering"
      ],
      "makeup": "minimal, natural or bare skin look"
    },
    "attire_constraints": {
      "source": "garment_from_input_reference_image",
      "preservation_rules": [
        "exact color dye and pattern",
        "exact fabric weave and texture",
        "exact thread stitching details",
        "exact fit, drape, and silhouette on the body"
      ],
      "modification_permission": "NONE"
    },
    "pose": {
      "framing": "full_body_standing",
      "style": "natural, relaxed, confident",
      "orientation": "facing camera to showcase garment front"
    }
  },
  "environment_definition": {
    "location_type": "outdoor_urban_sidewalk",
    "specific_context": "outside a stylish cafe or artisan building facade",
    "contextual_logic": "architecture and decor must visually complement the style of the reference clothing",
    "atmosphere": "elevated, authentic city life, cinematic quality",
    "background_elements": [
      "textured building materials (brick, stone, wood)",
      "cafe seating or planter boxes",
      "pavement textures"
    ]
  },
  "composition_and_layout": {
    "camera_principles": [
      "commercial fashion standards",
      "golden ratio alignment of subject",
      "product-centered focus",
      "grid alignment"
    ],
    "framing_scale": "wide full shot (head to toe)",
    "spatial_margins": {
      "top_margin": "generous clear space above head for potential typography/cropping",
      "side_margins": "balanced clear space",
      "bottom_margin": "clear space below feet"
    }
  },
  "lighting_and_optics": {
    "source": "natural daylight",
    "quality": "soft, diffused sunlight or open shade",
    "color_temperature": "warm undertones",
    "shadows": "clean, natural falloff defining form without harshness"
  },
  "constraints_and_prohibitions": {
    "must_not_render": [
      "airbrushed skin",
      "plastic textures",
      "studio backdrop",
      "altered clothing design",
      "overly posed look"
    ]
  }
}

### 186. 服装商品抠图贴纸提示词

> 一个图像编辑指令，要求 AI 从参考照片中分离并展平每件衣物，制作成剪纸贴纸，然后将它们放回图像中，并用手写文字进行标注，以营造时尚笔记本的美学效果。

![服装商品抠图贴纸提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967479204_nvxxhp_G-Ix5iubEAAcpex.jpg)

```
Collect each clothing item worn by the girl in the first photo and place them on top of the same photo as flat, cut-out stickers. Keep every piece neatly outlined like a collage sticker. Next to each stickered clothing item, write its name in a soft pencil-style handwritten label, creating an aesthetic fashion-notebook look.
```

### 190. 巨型泰迪熊时尚大片提示

**作者**: [Shanvi](https://x.com/Skurmii/status/2008377565296423244)  **日期**: 2026-01-06  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成逼真的时尚杂志摄影棚照片。它要求保留参考图像中的面部特征，指定拍摄对象的姿势（侧身坐着，抱着一个道具），服装（来自第二张参考图像中的确切服装，高跟鞋），以及道具本身：一个巨大的、150 厘米高的泰迪熊，所有这些都设置在无缝的纯粉色背景下，并采用高调照明。

### 197. Branded gifts postcard illustration prompt

**作者**: [AmirMušić](https://x.com/AmirMushich/status/2006795197087207618)  **日期**: 2026-01-01  **语言**: en

> A highly detailed prompt for generating a hand-drawn fashion illustration of a Christmas tree constructed from a chaotic stack of branded product boxes. It specifies composition, strict adherence to the brand's color palette and typography, and an 'Alcohol Marker and Ink' sketch art style on a white paper background.

![Branded gifts postcard illustration prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508443343_ivwzcs_G9mRaMhWcAAQc6T.jpg)

```
[A charming, hand-drawn fashion illustration of a Christmas tree constructed entirely from a chaotic stack of [{argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}] product boxes.

**COMPOSITION:**
The boxes are piled in a pyramid shape to mimic the silhouette of a Christmas tree. The boxes vary slightly in size and angle, creating a playful, unstable, organic look. At the very top, there is a simple golden star.

**BRAND PALETTE & AESTHETICS (CRITICAL):**
The boxes must be colored strictly according to [{argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}]'s official color palette (e.g., Tiffany Blue for Tiffany, Orange/Brown for Louis Vuitton, Red/White for Supreme).
* **Details:** Visible [{argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}] logos are printed on the sides of the boxes. Add realistic packaging details like small shipping labels, barcodes, and tape to enhance the "delivery box" vibe.

**ART STYLE (MARKER SKETCH):**
The image is NOT a 3D render. It is a high-quality "Alcohol Marker and Ink" sketch on white paper. The style is loose, artistic, and vibrant, typical of fashion design sketches. The colors have the texture of markers; the outlines are done in fine black ink.

**TYPOGRAPHY (STRICT BRAND MATCH):**
At the very bottom of the illustration, centered, write the phrase: "{argument name="holiday message" default="Happy New Year!"}".
1.  **Font Style:** The font must mimic the official typographic language of [{argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}] (e.g., if Nike: use a heavy Condensed Sans-Serif; if Gucci: use a refined Serif). The text style must feel like an extension of the brand's identity.
2.  **Size:** The text must be very small and discreet. It should occupy a maximum of 20% of the total image width.

**BACKGROUND:**
Clean white paper texture background.]
```

**Related**: [[品牌广告]]、[[综合产品]]、[[手绘素描]]

```
{
  "prompt_description": {
    "subject_details": {
      "gender": "Female",
        "color": "Platinum blonde",
        "style": "Messy high ponytail or updo",
      "expression": "Model-like pout, looking directly at the camera",
     "skin_features": "light skin tone with freckles",
      "pose": "Standing profile-forward, leaning slightly towards the vehicle, holding a gas nozzle"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "dress": "Strapless, voluminous baby {argument name="dress color" default="pink"} gown entirely covered in feathers (ostrich style), high-low hemline (mini in front, floor-length train in back)",

### 200. 魅惑之美口红广告文案提示

**作者**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin/status/2006372311306314152)  **日期**: 2025-12-31  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的美妆广告图片，画面中一位女性倚靠在一支巨大的、光泽感十足的红色 MAC 唇膏旁，强调专业的影棚灯光、奢华的化妆品美学，并带有一个手写的“Devilish Beauty”文字元素。

![魅惑之美口红广告文案提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456159819_qs7un9_G9gQrljWIAACrUb.jpg)

```
A high-end, hyper-realistic beauty advertisement shot.

Composition:
Side-view composition of an attractive brunette woman, positioned slightly in profile. She is leaning her back confidently against a gigantic red lipstick, scaled dramatically larger than life. Her arms are crossed, posture strong and elegant, while she turns her head to look directly at the camera with a bold, self-assured expression.

Appearance:
She has smooth, luminous skin, deep brown hair styled sleek and polished, and striking red lipstick that perfectly matches the oversized product behind her. Her facial features are symmetrical and refined, with confident eyes and a subtle, knowing gaze.
She wears a minimalist black dress, form-fitting, elegant, and timeless.

Product:
The oversized lipstick is bright red, glossy, perfectly cylindrical, clearly branded {argument name="brand" default="MAC"} with realistic logo placement and premium material finish.

Text Element:
At the top of the image, the slogan “{argument name="slogan" default="Devilish Beauty"}” is written as if handwritten with red lipstick—bold, sensual strokes, slightly imperfect, glossy texture, natural lipstick smudge edges.

Background:
Pure white studio background, seamless, high-key, no visible shadows or distractions.

Lighting:
Professional studio lighting—soft key light on her face, gentle rim light to define her silhouette, subtle reflections on the lipstick tube. Clean, luxury cosmetic ad lighting.

Style & Quality:
Ultra-photorealistic, luxury fashion photography, crisp focus, natural skin texture, premium cosmetics campaign aesthetic, editorial magazine quality.

Negative Prompt; anime, illustration, CGI, cartoon, flat lighting, low detail, blurry, distorted anatomy, plastic skin, over-smoothed face, low-budget ad, cluttered background
```

> 一个用于生成逼真的电商产品图片的结构化提示，具体来说，是一张中年女性穿着连衣裙的全身照。该提示严格要求使用上传的参考图片来精确呈现服装细节，并要求采用室内日光和智能手机相机瑕疵，以营造自然、随意的“顾客试穿”美感。

Preserve all garment details precisely: same color, fabric, stitching, seams, fit, silhouette, length, and texture. Do NOT stylize, redesign, or alter the clothing in any way.",
  
  "style": {
    "realism": "photorealistic",
    "aesthetic": "real customer try-on",
    "quality": "natural smartphone photo"
  },
  
  "camera": {
    "device": "modern smartphone",
    "framing": "full body with extra headroom and footroom",
    "angle": "straight-on or very slight natural angle",
    "imperfections": [
      "slight off-center framing",
      "minor tilt",
      "subtle depth blur"
    ]
  },
  
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural indoor daylight",
    "source": "window light",
    "quality": "soft, diffused",
    "tone": "neutral to slightly warm",
    "restriction": "no studio lights, no flash, no harsh shadows"
  },
  
  "model": {
    "body_type": "average, realistic",
    "skin": "visible natural skin texture with light blemishes",
    "face": "soft, age-appropriate facial features",
    "hair": "simple, natural, everyday styling",
    "makeup": "minimal or none",
    "expression": "casual, relaxed, authentic",
    "pose": "natural standing posture, not posed or editorial"
  },
  
  "environment": {
    "location": "woman’s home interior",

### 209. 黑白魅力摄影提示词，适用于 Nano Banana Pro

**作者**: [Bananai](https://x.com/aibananai/status/2005318420082884910)  **日期**: 2025-12-28  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 模型设计的高度详细、结构化的提示，用于生成一张黑白、高对比度的魅力照片。场景设定在一架豪华电梯内，捕捉到一位女性主体正在镜子中检查自己的倒影，利用硬光、机载闪光灯照明，营造出戏剧性的复古好莱坞黑色电影美学。

![黑白魅力摄影提示词，适用于 Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061694281_cs5nfi_G9RSdyIX0AAZ5ui.jpg)
![黑白魅力摄影提示词，适用于 Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061694543_etxtac_G9RSdyKWoAA7RZc.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "quality": "ultra_photorealistic, raw film scan",
    "resolution": "8k",
    "camera": "Analog 35mm camera with direct flash",
    "lens": "35mm",
    "style": "Black and white glamour photography, high-contrast flash, celebrity candid, vintage Hollywood noir meets modern luxury, grainy film texture"
  },

  "scene": {
    "location": "Luxury elevator interior",
    "environment": [
      "mirrored walls reflecting the subject",
      "Art Deco style fluted columns",
      "elevator control panel with illuminated buttons in background",
      "metallic surfaces",
      "claustrophobic but glamorous space"
    ],
    "time": "night / event after-party",
    "atmosphere": "intimate, exclusive, high-fashion, vintage glam, paparazzi flash aesthetic"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "Direct on-camera flash (hard lighting)",
    "key_light": "frontal flash creating bright specular highlights on forehead and chest",
    "contrast": "high contrast monochrome",
    "shadows": "sharp, deep shadows behind the subject due to flash",
    "effect": "sparkle on sequins, glossy reflection on skin, dramatic vintage noir vibe"
  },

  "camera_perspective": {
    "pov": "Over-the-shoulder shot",
    "focus": "Sharp focus on the reflection in the mirror, foreground (back of head) slightly blurred",
    "framing": "Upper body and reflection",
    "composition": "Subject's back in foreground, face visible in the mirror reflection"
  },

  "subject": {
    "gender": "{argument name="gender" default="female"}",
    "age": "20s",
    "ethnicity": "Caucasian",
    "body": {
      "type": "fit and curvy",
      "skin": "pale, high-gloss finish from flash, realistic texture with pores visible (no plastic smoothing)",
      "chest": "cleavage visible through keyhole cutout"
    },

    "hair": {
      "style": "slicked-back distinct sculptural bun",
      "details": "highly stylized 'kiss curl' or gelled swirl plastered on forehead",
      "texture": "glossy, wet-look styling products",
      "color": "blonde (rendered in light grey/white in B&W)"
    },

    "face": {
      "expression": "seductive, dazed glamour, mouth slightly open",
      "eyes": "heavy winged eyeliner, looking slightly downwards or at self in mirror",
      "lips": "full, glossy lipstick, finger touching lower lip",
      "makeup": "heavy evening glam, defined eyebrows, sculpted contours"
    },

    "hands": {
      "position": "Right hand raised touching mouth/chin area",
      "details": "long manicured nails (almond shape), large diamond ring on ring finger"
    },

    "pose": {
      "orientation": "Standing facing the mirror",
      "head": "tilted slightly back and to the side",
      "interaction": "checking appearance/makeup in the elevator mirror",
      "vibe": "caught in the moment, cinematic"
    },

    "outfit": {
      "main_piece": {
        "type": "{argument name="outfit type" default="Haute couture beaded evening gown"}",
        "material": "heavy sequins an"
    }
  }
}
```

### 210. 蓝色时分下的冬季街头时尚大片

> 一个提示，用于生成一张年轻女性的视觉图像，她身穿露肩短款上衣和破洞牛仔裤，站在白雪覆盖的居民街道上，时值蓝色时刻（黄昏）。场景强调了暴露的服装与寒冷、宁静的冬季氛围之间的对比，并使用柔和、漫射的自然光。

        "fabric": "Ribbed texture",

          "Twisted knot at the bust",
          "Pointed/handkerchief hemline",
          "Sweetheart neckline"
        ]

        "type": "Jeans",

          "Large distressed rips on thighs",
          "fitted waist"
        ]

### 211. 超逼真的街头风生活方式照片

> 一个用于生成以奢侈品牌店面为背景的高端街头风格时尚照片的结构化提示。当您希望图像模型能够产生一致、可艺术指导的结果时，它会非常有用——以清晰的规范格式涵盖模特的造型、服装风格、姿势、地点细节和灯光。

{

    "demographic": "Young woman",
    "appearance": {
      "skin_tone": "Tanned / Bronzed",
      "hair": {
        "color": "Dark brown",
        "style": "Long, voluminous, wavy, loose",
        "parting": "Side part"
      },

      "color": "Black with white grid/check pattern",
      "details": [
        "Gold buttons",
        "White trim/piping",
        "Collarless",
        "Structured shoulders"
      ]
    },
    "top": {
      "item": "Turtleneck sweater",
      "color": "White",
      "material": "Fitted knit"
    },
    "bottom": {
      "item": "Pleated mini skirt",
      "color": "Black",
      "style": "High-waisted, tennis skirt style"
    },
    "footwear": {
      "item": "Knee-high boots",
      "color": "Black",
      "material": "Leather"
    }
  },
  "accessories": {
    "eyewear": {
      "item": "Sunglasses",
      "style": "Black, oversized, rectangular/cat-eye hybrid"
    },
    "handbag": {
      "item": "Top-handle handbag",
      "brand_indicator": "Gold interlocking 'CC' logo",
      "material": "Black leather",
      "shape": "Structured, rectangular"
    },
    "jewelry": "Minimal/Not visible"
  },
  "pose": {
    "stance": "Standing walking pose",
    "left_hand": "Touching sunglasses/hair lightly",
    "right_hand": "Holding handbag by the handle at side",
    "orientation": "Facing forward"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Luxury storefront exterior",
    "architecture": {
      "facade": "Black wood/metal with large glass windows",
      "signage": "Gold 'CHANEL' lettering above door and on windows"
    },
    "elements": [
      "Mannequins in window display wearing black",
      "Grey paved sidewalk/stone tiles"
    ]

### 215. 高端时尚动感飞跃商业提示词

**作者**: [Toxic Latent](https://x.com/Toxic_Latent_pp/status/2004829803908874606)  **日期**: 2025-12-27  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张动态的、高级时装商业图片，描绘一位女性正在优雅地跳跃。该提示指定了低角度拍摄，背景是晴朗的蓝天，鲜艳飘逸的织物在她周围翻腾。它要求强烈的太阳逆光、鲜明的主色调和电影般的色彩分级，旨在营造一种令人惊叹、欣快的情绪，适合香水广告。

{
  "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
  "meta_data": {
    "concept": "Dynamic High-Fashion Leap",
    "mood": "Elegant, Vivid, Euphoric, Breathtaking Beauty"
  },
  "subject_details": {
    "character": "Stunningly beautiful woman, dancer-like grace",
    "action": "A massive, graceful leap into the air, arms extended",
    "shot_type": "Low angle looking up against the sky",
    "details": "Metres of flowing, vibrant fabric (e.g., bright {argument name="fabric color" default="yellow or royal blue"} silk) billowing dramatically around her like wings. Hair flowing beautifully in the wind",
    "expression": "Ecstatic, beautiful wide smile looking up towards the sun, flawless face"
  },
  "environment_context": {
    "location": "Cliff edge or vast open landscape high up",
    "background_elements": "Incredibly clear, saturated blue sky with endless horizon. Strong sunlight",
    "atmosphere": "Freedom, majesty, vibrant energy"
  },
  "lighting_setup": {
    "type": "Strong Sun Backlight",
    "source": "Direct sun",
    "effects": "Making the translucent fabric glow, rim lighting on hair and body. High contrast but flattering on face",
    "color_grading": "Ultra-vivid primary colors, commercial cinematic look, sharp clarity",
    "style": "High-end commercial photography (like a perfume ad)"
  },
  "camera_specification": {
    "body": "Canon EOS R5",
    "lens": "24-70mm F2.8",

    "style": "Dynamic beauty editorial"
  },

    "resolution": "8k",

    "focus": "Sharp on the face and body in mid-air"
  },

### 216. 高级定制时尚：华丽礼服的编辑特写

**作者**: [KeorUnreal](https://x.com/KeorUnreal/status/2004659391811793275)  **日期**: 2025-12-26  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张 8K 超现实、高端的时尚编辑照片：一位惊艳的女性（面部严格遵循参考图像）优雅地斜倚在城堡环境中一张质朴的贵妃榻上。重点是她那件华丽的露肩深红色美人鱼礼服，以及电影般的双色调灯光（忧郁的青色和温暖的琥珀色）。

![高级定制时尚：华丽礼服的编辑特写](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988079936_sjv9x3_G9H7FpYW8AAQ35Y.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "meta": {
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "resolution": "8K ultra-high-resolution",
      "realism_level": "Photorealistic, ultra realistic details"
    },
    "artistic_style": {
      "genre": "High-end editorial fashion photograph",
      "atmosphere": "Luxurious, cinematic",
      "shot_type": "Captive shot"
    },
    "subject": {
      "constraint": "Use same face and figure 100 percent as uploaded image",
      "general": "Stunning woman",
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "color": "White",
          "texture": Straight",
          "volume": "Voluminous",
          "length": "Long"
        },
        "makeup": {
          "finish": "Glamorous matte",
          "eye_style": "Blue eyes"
        }
      },
      "pose_and_expression": {
        "posture": "Gracefully reclining",
        "hand_position": "One hand touching her hair",
        "expression": "Serene",
        "eyes": "Open"
      }
    },
    "attire": {
      "garment_type": "Gown",
      "silhouette": "Mermaid",
      "neckline": "Off-the-shoulder",
      "color": "{argument name="gown color" default="Cremisi"}",
      "details": {
        "bodice": {
          "style": "Open Corset-style midriff",
          "material": "Mesh",
          "structural_element": "Vertical boning"
        },
        "sleeves": {
          "adornment": "Delicate beaded fringe"
        },
        "embellishments": {
          "intensity": "Heavily embellished",
          "style": "Intricate",
          "materials": [
            "Silver sequins",
            "Pearls",
            "Crystals"
          ]
        }
      }

The DJ decks feature intricate knobs and platters carved from clear blue ice, exhibiting subsurface scattering and prismatic light refraction. A stylish female DJ wears high-end avant-garde après-ski fashion (white faux fur, reflective oversized goggles) and is actively mixing on the frozen equipment. Behind her, a dramatic, massive snow avalanche cascades down a granite mountain face, captured with slight motion blur to emphasize speed. The lighting is harsh midday alpine sun, creating sharp shadows, blinding specular highlights on the wet ice, and atmospheric snow dust. ### 225. 高影响力男士时尚专题：身份锁定

**作者**: [Soner 🇹🇷͜͜͡͡✯](https://x.com/SonerOzdemir35/status/2003397361226101234)  **日期**: 2025-12-23  **语言**: en

> 一个高度受限的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张具有高影响力、聚焦男模的时尚社论快照。它强制严格保留上传图片中的身份，详细描述了拍摄对象的自信表情、健硕体格、深色服装（高领上衣、定制长裤），以及在欧洲街景中采用冷色调、高角度构图的特点。

![高影响力男士时尚专题：身份锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766673220163_4j3lnt_G812G3iXcAAxED4.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "high-impact fashion editorial, cinematic social snapshot",

  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_uploaded_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,
    "facial_structure_consistency_priority": true,
    "subject_face_embedding_preserved": true,
    "no_morphing": true,
    "no_face_blending": true,
    "notes": "Keep the man from the attached image as the main character. Preserve his facial features, proportions, and overall identity exactly as in the reference."
  },

  "subject": {
    "gender": "male",
    "role": "main character / fashion editorial model",
    "build": "athletic, broad shoulders, strong masculine frame",
    "expression": {
      "eyes": {
        "look": "sharp, piercing gaze directed at camera",
        "energy": "confident, cold, dominant"
      },
      "mouth": {
        "position": "relaxed lips, subtle controlled smirk",
        "energy": "chic, self-assured"
      },
      "overall": "high-impact, charismatic presence"
    },
    "face": {
      "preserve_original": true,
      "makeup": "none",
      "skin": "natural texture, no beauty filters",
      "style": "cool-toned masculine editorial"
    },
    "hair": {
      "style": "natural male hairstyle from face model",
      "effect": "clean, sharp, high-fashion finish"
    },
    "body": {
      "frame": "athletic, powerful upper body",
      "pose": {
        "position": "leaning forward slightly",
        "overall": "dynamic foreshortening emphasizing head and upper torso"
      },
      "skin": {
        "tone": "natural light-to-medium",
        "lighting_effect": "even, cool daylight with soft contrast"
      }
    },
    "clothing": {
      "top": {
        "type": "ultra-fine knit or fitted structured top",
        "color": "cool grey or charcoal (no white)",
        "details": "mock neck or clean crew, slim fit",
        "effect": "sharp silhouette, masculine lines"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "tailored dark trousers",
        "details": "high waist, clean luxury cut, no belt visible"
      }
    }
  },

  "photography": {
    "camera_style": "high-end social media editorial snapshot",
    "angle": "high angle POV",
    "shot_type": "medium close-up",
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "texture": "clear, sharp, natural skin detail",
    "lighting": "cool overcast daylight, soft diffuse light"
  },

  "background": {
    "setting": "European classic architecture",
    "atmosphere": "fashionable street corner",
    "blur": "controlled bokeh background emphasizing subject"
  },

  "constraints": [
    "Do not change the man's face or identity",
    "Keep facial proportions identical to reference",
    "No accessories (no jewelry, no watch, no sunglasses)",
    "Dark clothing only (no white)",
    "Avoid feminine styling",
    "No beauty filters"
  ],

  "negative_prompt": [
    "female body",
    "feminine features"
  ]
}

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 提示，用于生成一个视觉上引人注目的吸睛图片（缩略图/横幅），该图片结合了企业科技设计和日本动漫艺术。它采用对角线分割布局，左侧以黑黄色调展示文字内容（标题、副标题、行动号召），右侧则是一幅可爱的未来派动漫女孩插画。

```
metadata:
model_context: "Corporate Tech, High-Energy Business Youtube Thumbnail mixed with Anime Art"

image_structure:
composition_type: "Diagonal Split Layout (Arrowhead Shape)"
visual_flow: "Left Text (Problem/Solution) -> Right Visual (Result/Character)"
layers:
layer_background_left:
shape: "Geometric polygon covering left 60% of screen, with a sharp arrow-point extending into the right side"
color: "Matte Black (#1A1A1A)"
texture: "Subtle carbon fiber or mesh pattern to add tech depth"
layer_typography:

location: "Centered within the left black area"
alignment: "Left-aligned or Centered"
elements:
- type: "Headline (Main)"
text: "{argument name="メイン見出し" default="AI副業で\n稼ぐデザイン"}"
style: "Extremely bold, heavy Gothic font (Impact style). White text."
highlight: "Apply Bright Yellow (#FFD700) color to the word '稼ぐ' (Earn) and 'AI'"
- type: "Sub-Headline (Detail)"
text: "{argument name="サブ見出し" default="Nano Banana Pro完全攻略"}"
style: "Smaller white sans-serif text, clean and readable"
- type: "Body Text (Explanation)"
text: "{argument name="説明文" default="未経験からプロのクオリティへ。\n最短ルートで収益化を目指す講座。"}"
style: "Small, thin grey or white text block, justified layout"
layer_cta_button:
shape: "Rounded Pill Shape"
color: "Bright Yellow (#FFD700)"

text: "{argument name="CTAテキスト" default="今すぐ申し込む ▶"}"
text_color: "Black"
location: "Bottom left, below the text block"
style: "Flat design with slight drop shadow"
layer_visual_right:
shape: "Fills the remaining right side (behind the arrow overlap)"
content: "Japanese Kawaii Anime Girl illustration"

style: "2D Cel-shaded anime art, high detail, vibrant colors"
details:
subject: "A cute anime girl with a futuristic / cyber-fashion look"
appearance:
hair: "Pastel pink and blue gradient bob cut, with cyber hair clips"
eyes: "Large sparkling anime eyes, confident smile"
clothing: "Stylish tech-wear hoodie with yellow accents to match the background theme"

### 233. 高级时装圣诞专题提示

**作者**: [Javeriya ✨](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281/status/2002388800425898354)  **日期**: 2025-12-20  **语言**: en

> 为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 3.0 设计的、高度结构化且细节丰富的提示，旨在生成一张华丽的圣诞节高级时装专题图片，画面中模特身着红色天鹅绒高级定制礼服，置身于深勃艮第色背景前，点缀着摄影棚雪花和金属饰品。

![高级时装圣诞专题提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385991594_7i2tcz_G8nqAGAbMAQYwhK.jpg)

```
[Identity_Preservation]

### 235. Kickstarter 众筹活动生成器提示

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2002330135748346099)  **日期**: 2025-12-20  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的系统提示，指示模型扮演高级产品设计师和众筹活动经理的角色。它分析输入图像的材料特性，自动选择并生成一个现代智能可穿戴设备（夹克、背包或运动鞋）的概念，然后以适合 Kickstarter 众筹页面的精确 2x2 网格布局可视化该概念，包括一张主视觉图、一张细节图、一张生活方式图和一张众筹 UI 模拟图。

![Kickstarter 众筹活动生成器提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385957583_svruzw_G8VpVYbXAAYij7H.jpg)

```
Act as a Senior Product Designer and Crowdfunding Campaign Manager.

1. ANALYZE INPUT
Look at the attached image. Determine the material properties (Soft vs. Hard), the primary colors, and the texture.

2. AUTO-SELECT SMART WEARABLE
Use this logic to choose the product category. The goal is Clean Modern Tech, not Cyberpunk.

IF the input is Soft or Fabric-like ({argument name="soft input examples" default="Ramen, Towel, Moss"})
GENERATE: The All-Climate Smart Jacket.
Features: Self-regulating temperature control, hydrophobic coating based on the input texture, and hidden magnetic pockets.

IF the input is Rigid, Boxy, or Container-like ({argument name="rigid input examples" default="Toaster, Book, Suitcase"})
GENERATE: The Ultimate Commuter Backpack.
Features: Integrated power bank with solar coating, anti-theft biometric zipper locks, and organized modular compartments.

IF the input is Mechanical or Footwear-shaped ({argument name="mechanical input examples" default="Stapler, Car, Tool"})
GENERATE: The Urban Mobility Smart Sneaker.
Features: Energy-returning sole technology, step-tracking sensors embedded in the heel, and auto-tensioning laces.

3. EXECUTE VISUALIZATION (2x2 GRID)
Generate a single image split into a precise 2x2 grid layout.

Top Left Panel (Hero Shot):
A clean, studio-lit 3/4 angle view of the product on a white or light grey background. It must look refined and manufacturable, using the texture of the input image as a premium material.

Top Right Panel (Detail Shot):
A zoomed-in macro shot focusing on a specific high-tech feature (e.g., a USB-C port, a magnetic buckle, or a waterproof seam) that shows off the input texture quality.

Bottom Left Panel (Lifestyle Shot):
A photorealistic shot of a fashionable model wearing the item in a clean, modern city setting (daytime). They look comfortable and stylish.

Bottom Right Panel (Campaign UI):
A mockup of a Kickstarter campaign page. It should show the product title, a green progress bar at 100% funded, and a bright green button that says Back This Project.

Overall Style: High-key lighting, soft shadows, 8k resolution, commercial product photography, minimalist design aesthetic.
```

{
  "image_analysis": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with long, straight brunette hair.",
      "expression": "Neutral to confident gaze, looking directly at the camera.",

    },

      "item": "White mini dress.",
      "style": "Spaghetti straps, fitted bodice, flowy pleated skirt (skater dress style), lightweight fabric."
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Modern interior space.",
      "elements": [
        "Grey wall with vertical alignment.",
        "Large geometric mirror (diamond/diagonal cuts) reflecting the subject's back.",
        "Vertical wall-mounted light fixture."
      ]
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Ambient and moody.",
      "colors": "Warm orange/reddish glow from the wall light, contrasting with cooler grey tones of the wall.",
      "shadows": "Soft shadows, highlighting the contours of the dress and legs."
    },
    "composition": {
      "framing": "Full body shot.",
      "perspective": "Eye-level.",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on the subject, clear reflection in the mirror."
    }
  },
  "generation_prompt": "A photorealistic full-body shot of a young woman with long {argument name="hair color" default="brown"} hair leaning against a {argument name="wall color" default="grey"} wall, wearing a short {argument name="dress color" default="white"} sleeveless mini dress with a flowy skirt. ### 246. Y2K 可爱时尚画报提示

**作者**: [Glitter Gal](https://x.com/GlitterPixely/status/1998248367395066178)  **日期**: 2025-12-09  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成多面板、风格一致的 Y2K 卡哇伊时尚编辑图片，重点关注超广角透视、超女性化美学，以及模特的特定服装和生物特征。

```
{
  "meta_control": {
    "generation_mode": "multi_panel_consistent",
    "priority_stack": ["identity_lock", "perspective_physics", "material_fidelity", "environmental_coherence"],
    "quality_target": "editorial_print_ready"
  },

    "secondary": "Technical demonstration of foreshortening in a hyper-feminine aesthetic",
    "publication_context": "Double-page spread, pop-culture magazine collage layout"
  },
  "frame": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "layout": {
      "type": "2x2 grid collage",
      "gutter_width": "2px pink or seamless",
      "panel_uniformity": "identical dimensions per panel"
    }
  },
  "subject": {
    "type": "Human female fashion model",
    "identity_lock": {
      "enforcement_level": "strict",
      "anchor_features": ["face_geometry", "skin_tone", "body_proportions", "hair_color"]
    },
    "biometrics": {
      "age_presentation": "20-24",
      "height_cm": 170,
      "build": "Slender, petite model frame",
      "ethnicity_presentation": "Caucasian / Northern European features"
    },
    "facial_signature": {
      "structure": "Soft oval face shape, full cheeks, rounded feminine jawline",
      "eyes": "Large, expressive, bright blue, defined lashes with rhinestone accents",
      "nose": "Small, delicate button nose, slightly upturned",
      "lips": "Very full, plush and pillowy, glossy bubblegum pink",
      "skin": "Porcelain fair, smooth texture, heavy blush on nose and cheeks, highlighter glow",
      "expression_default": "Playful cute, duck face, winking, blowing kiss"
    },
    "hair": {
      "style": "Long golden blonde hair, half-up pigtails with fluffy scrunchies",
      "texture": "Silky, voluminous, crimped sections",
      "behavior": "Bouncing, dynamic movement"
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "jacket": {
        "item": "Cropped faux-fur jacket",
        "material": "High-pile mongolian fur",
        "color": "Pastel baby pink",

      },
      "top": {
